PS C:\WINDOWS\system32> # HAMLET PROJECT - CANDIDATE DATA VALIDATION
>> # Validate and reconcile the master candidate lists
>>
>> $dataPath = "E:\HamletUnified"
>> $reportPath = "E:\HamletUnified\DATA_VALIDATION_REPORT_$(Get-Date -Format 'yyyyMMdd_HHmmss').txt"
>>
>> Write-Host "========================================" -ForegroundColor Cyan
>> Write-Host "CANDIDATE DATA VALIDATION" -ForegroundColor Cyan
>> Write-Host "========================================`n" -ForegroundColor Cyan
>>
>> $report = @"
>> HAMLET PROJECT - DATA VALIDATION REPORT
>> Generated: $(Get-Date -Format 'yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss')
>>
>> ========================================
>> MASTER CANDIDATE FILE ANALYSIS
>> ========================================
>>
>> "@
>>
>> # Define the three critical files
>> $files = @{
>>     'Original' = 'ElectionCandidates_Original.csv'
>>     'English' = 'ElectionCandidates_English.csv'
>>     'Kurdish_Arabic' = 'لۆڤلی (2).csv'
>> }
>>
>> $fileData = @{}
>>
>> foreach ($key in $files.Keys) {
>>     $fileName = $files[$key]
>>     Write-Host "[ANALYZING] $fileName..." -ForegroundColor Yellow
>>
>>     # Search for the file
>>     $filePath = Get-ChildItem -Path $dataPath -Recurse -Filter $fileName -File -ErrorAction SilentlyContinue | Select-Object -First 1
>>
>>     if ($filePath) {
>>         Write-Host "  [FOUND] $($filePath.FullName)" -ForegroundColor Green
>>
>>         try {
>>             # Read the file
>>             $content = Import-Csv -Path $filePath.FullName -Encoding UTF8
>>             $rowCount = $content.Count
>>             $columns = $content[0].PSObject.Properties.Name
>>
>>             $fileData[$key] = @{
>>                 Path = $filePath.FullName
>>                 Rows = $rowCount
>>                 Columns = $columns
>>                 Data = $content
>>             }
>>
>>             $report += "`n[$key FILE]`n"
>>             $report += "  Path: $($filePath.FullName)`n"
>>             $report += "  Rows: $rowCount`n"
>>             $report += "  Columns ($($columns.Count)): $($columns -join ', ')`n"
>>
>>             Write-Host "  [OK] $rowCount rows, $($columns.Count) columns" -ForegroundColor White
>>
>>             # Sample first row
>>             $report += "  Sample Row 1:`n"
>>             foreach ($col in $columns | Select-Object -First 5) {
>>                 $value = $content[0].$col
>>                 if ($value.Length -gt 50) { $value = $value.Substring(0, 50) + "..." }
>>                 $report += "    - $col = $value`n"
>>             }
>>
>>         } catch {
>>             Write-Host "  [ERROR] Failed to read: $($_.Exception.Message)" -ForegroundColor Red
>>             $report += "`n[$key FILE] - ERROR: Unable to read`n"
>>         }
>>     } else {
>>         Write-Host "  [NOT FOUND] $fileName" -ForegroundColor Red
>>         $report += "`n[$key FILE] - NOT FOUND`n"
>>     }
>> }
>>
>> # Analysis
>> $report += "`n========================================`n"
>> $report += "DATA RECONCILIATION ANALYSIS`n"
>> $report += "========================================`n"
>>
>> if ($fileData.ContainsKey('Original') -and $fileData.ContainsKey('English')) {
>>     $originalRows = $fileData['Original'].Rows
>>     $englishRows = $fileData['English'].Rows
>>     $difference = $originalRows - $englishRows
>>
>>     $report += "`nRow Count Comparison:`n"
>>     $report += "  Original: $originalRows rows`n"
>>     $report += "  English:  $englishRows rows`n"
>>     $report += "  Difference: $difference rows`n"
>>
>>     Write-Host "`n[ANALYSIS] Row difference: $difference" -ForegroundColor Yellow
>>
>>     if ($difference -gt 0) {
>>         $report += "`n[FINDING] Original has $difference MORE rows than English`n"
>>         $report += "Possible reasons:`n"
>>         $report += "  1. Original contains duplicates`n"
>>         $report += "  2. English translation is incomplete`n"
>>         $report += "  3. Original includes multiple elections`n"
>>         $report += "  4. Data cleaning removed rows from English version`n"
>>     }
>>
>>     # Check for duplicates in Original
>>     Write-Host "[CHECKING] Duplicates in Original file..." -ForegroundColor Yellow
>>     $originalData = $fileData['Original'].Data
>>
>>     # Try to find ID or unique identifier column
>>     $idColumns = @('ID', 'CandidateID', 'ElectionNumber', 'Number', 'Candidate_ID')
>>     $idColumn = $null
>>
>>     foreach ($col in $idColumns) {
>>         if ($fileData['Original'].Columns -contains $col) {
>>             $idColumn = $col
>>             break
>>         }
>>     }
>>
>>     if ($idColumn) {
>>         $uniqueIds = ($originalData | Select-Object -Property $idColumn -Unique).Count
>>         $totalIds = $originalData.Count
>>         $duplicates = $totalIds - $uniqueIds
>>
>>         $report += "`nDuplicate Analysis (using column: $idColumn):`n"
>>         $report += "  Total rows: $totalIds`n"
>>         $report += "  Unique IDs: $uniqueIds`n"
>>         $report += "  Duplicates: $duplicates`n"
>>
>>         Write-Host "  [RESULT] $duplicates duplicate rows found" -ForegroundColor $(if ($duplicates -gt 0) { "Red" } else { "Green" })
>>
>>         if ($duplicates -gt 0) {
>>             $report += "`n[WARNING] Found $duplicates duplicate candidates!`n"
>>             $report += "Action needed: Deduplicate Original file`n"
>>         }
>>     } else {
>>         $report += "`n[WARNING] No standard ID column found. Cannot check duplicates automatically.`n"
>>         $report += "Available columns: $($fileData['Original'].Columns -join ', ')`n"
>>     }
>> }
>>
>> # Column comparison
>> if ($fileData.ContainsKey('Original') -and $fileData.ContainsKey('English')) {
>>     $origCols = $fileData['Original'].Columns
>>     $engCols = $fileData['English'].Columns
>>
>>     $report += "`n========================================`n"
>>     $report += "COLUMN STRUCTURE COMPARISON`n"
>>     $report += "========================================`n"
>>
>>     $report += "`nOriginal columns ($($origCols.Count)): $($origCols -join ', ')`n"
>>     $report += "`nEnglish columns ($($engCols.Count)): $($engCols -join ', ')`n"
>>
>>     # Find differences
>>     $onlyInOriginal = $origCols | Where-Object { $engCols -notcontains $_ }
>>     $onlyInEnglish = $engCols | Where-Object { $origCols -notcontains $_ }
>>
>>     if ($onlyInOriginal) {
>>         $report += "`nColumns ONLY in Original: $($onlyInOriginal -join ', ')`n"
>>     }
>>     if ($onlyInEnglish) {
>>         $report += "`nColumns ONLY in English: $($onlyInEnglish -join ', ')`n"
>>     }
>> }
>>
>> # Recommendations
>> $report += "`n========================================`n"
>> $report += "DIRECTOR'S RECOMMENDATIONS`n"
>> $report += "========================================`n"
>>
>> if ($fileData.ContainsKey('Original')) {
>>     $report += "`n[RECOMMENDATION] Master Data Source:`n"
>>
>>     if ($fileData['Original'].Rows -gt 10000) {
>>         $report += "  - Use ElectionCandidates_Original.csv as PRIMARY source`n"
>>         $report += "  - Action: Check for and remove duplicates if found`n"
>>         $report += "  - Expected final count: ~7,770 unique candidates`n"
>>     }
>>
>>     if ($fileData.ContainsKey('English')) {
>>         $report += "`n[RECOMMENDATION] Bilingual Strategy:`n"
>>         $report += "  - Original.csv = Arabic/Kurdish names (authoritative)`n"
>>         $report += "  - English.csv = Translated names for outreach`n"
>>         $report += "  - Action: Merge both files with ID matching`n"
>>         $report += "  - Result: One master file with both language versions`n"
>>     }
>> }
>>
>> $report += "`n[NEXT STEPS]`n"
>> $report += "1. Review this validation report`n"
>> $report += "2. Deduplicate Original file if needed`n"
>> $report += "3. Merge Original + English into master bilingual file`n"
>> $report += "4. Proceed with MVP testing`n"
>> $report += "5. Begin social media collection on clean master file`n"
>>
>> # Save report
>> $report | Out-File -FilePath $reportPath -Encoding UTF8
>>
>> Write-Host "`n========================================" -ForegroundColor Cyan
>> Write-Host "VALIDATION COMPLETE!" -ForegroundColor Green
>> Write-Host "========================================" -ForegroundColor Cyan
>> Write-Host "Report saved to: $reportPath" -ForegroundColor Yellow
>> Write-Host ""
>>
>> # Open report
>> Start-Process notepad.exe $reportPath
========================================
CANDIDATE DATA VALIDATION
========================================

[ANALYZING] ElectionCandidates_English.csv...
  [FOUND] E:\HamletUnified\clean_election_data\ElectionCandidates_English.csv
  [OK] 7769 rows, 8 columns
[ANALYZING] ElectionCandidates_Original.csv...

WARNING: One or more headers were not specified. Default names starting with "H" have been used in
place of any missing headers.
  [OK] 7769 rows, 10 columns
[ANALYZING] لۆڤلی (2).csv...
  [FOUND] E:\HamletUnified\لۆڤلی (2).csv
  [OK] 7769 rows, 8 columns

[ANALYSIS] Row difference: 0
[CHECKING] Duplicates in Original file...

========================================
VALIDATION COMPLETE!

Report saved to: E:\HamletUnified\DATA_VALIDATION_REPORT_20251015_005227.txt
